If any of the\\n29: # properties are modified, applications should be restarted to ensure the\\n30: # changes are properly reflected.\\n31: #\\n32: # The special \\\"include\\\" property can be defined one or multiple times with\\n33: # a filesystem path value. The effect of each definition is to include a\\n34: # referred security properties file inline, adding all its properties.\\n35: # Security properties defined before an include statement may be overridden\\n36: # by properties in the included file, if their names match. Conversely,\\n37: # properties defined after an include statement may override properties in\\n38: # the included file.\\n39: #\\n40: # Included files, as well as files pointed to by java.security.properties,\\n41: # can include other files recursively. Paths may be absolute or relative.\\n42: # Each relative path is resolved against the base file containing its\\n43: # \\\"include\\\" definition, if local. Paths may contain system properties for\\n44: # expansion in the form of ${system.property}.
